Kutupa I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ tombo mina꞉la꞉ alema꞉ handeke tolo kitolo alota꞉ Mo Koda꞉na꞉ tembolo da make mo oloda yaapo pua tombo mie laata꞉ mo tembolo da pa꞉ta꞉ yeni piteleme wanda꞉hali yata꞉pea꞉peke lea꞉me.
Pate mo hama꞉ nane momba꞉la꞉la꞉ hama꞉ manuta꞉ tombo na mia꞉pe lea꞉me. Pa ekipeke koto ekita꞉ mo pi na miniki haleme tapake pa꞉ta꞉ hala꞉la꞉ hama꞉e lea꞉me. Koto tapakema꞉ta꞉ kaisepo halitieke yaapona꞉ paa yaapona꞉ mo yakopiki daoni lu tumbalimikie.
Kutupa I̱ma꞉ yaka wekitisi hali yaapo mo palaowamanu mondu hala꞉ ekima꞉ dau yamao 1 daoseni kutupa 260 natemanu Koda꞉na꞉ pi walawaena꞉ tapaalueke lea꞉me.
Mo wekitisi hali yaapota꞉ mo olipi ti yaapo pita꞉ ola꞉pake keo panka꞉la꞉ ale yaapoe. Ipilikita꞉ mo kenke Tekehalina꞉ puki tikitiki halepeme.
Ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ koto hali yaapo hoeyaaluekema꞉ pimika꞉na꞉ta꞉ ti uleke ipilika꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ opolu bao mo ipilika꞉ a꞉nda꞉ tunkiliki haliweki hoeyaalieke. Kutupa dupilipi ekima꞉ta꞉ mo hali yaapo hoeyaaluekema꞉ taapilimi wanda꞉halita꞉ lilieke.
Ipilikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo Koda꞉na꞉ pi laaso halipi natena꞉ lako na epena꞉ laa oli ya a꞉mbolota꞉ honkopu ula꞉me. Kutupa make mo opolo hala꞉ ikali manuta꞉ we au lena꞉ loluekema꞉ make ane mone yeni ki ipilika꞉ hone pa꞉la꞉ tupa꞉ do kenke a꞉pa hoeyaena꞉ laa make honkopu ula꞉me.
Ipilikana꞉ma꞉ ipilika꞉ pi walo paeyaalipi natena꞉ta꞉ mo honiki na wiki naku tieke kiake pa꞉ta꞉ hao opulu baalia꞉ sayalema꞉ handeke ale tieke hombelekema꞉ mo hali yaapo ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ pilieke. Mo alema꞉ta꞉ mo hali yaapo bepolao lu homaota꞉
ipilika꞉ tokota꞉ ipilika꞉ Tekehali lu endiaemeke daoni tiekena꞉ pota꞉na꞉ pa wina꞉ lelieke. Koto daonita꞉ onkoluma꞉ ala꞉ biki yaapota꞉ Sodomo pita꞉ Idiepi yaapo ula꞉me.
Kapomani ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ handeteke hala꞉ kenkemanu make tapake ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ make pi ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ make tutu ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ make paeyaoma꞉ mo hali yaapona꞉ tokota꞉ nate tepona꞉ nate ma꞉nda꞉na꞉ tukikina꞉ta꞉ handolo make na hoina꞉ lelimikie.
Pa ekipeke do kenkena꞉ haleme wanda꞉halima꞉ta꞉ mo hali yaapo homelepe ekina꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homilimikie. Kutupa ne pambolo hata꞉ pa hala꞉la꞉ alemanu ika꞉ ika꞉ kone anemone tapa alu alu pilimikie. Pa ekipeke mo potopede hali yaapoma꞉ta꞉ wanda꞉hali pa꞉ta꞉ tanda tieke mea epepeme laa lelimikie.
Koto nate tepo paeya nate ma꞉nda꞉na꞉ tukikina꞉ta꞉ da꞉ta꞉la꞉eki hala꞉la꞉ pomo Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ a꞉pa mo hali yaapo pa꞉ta꞉ honda꞉ pambeeketa꞉ mo hali yaapo tialu pipime. Kutupa mo hali yaapo handeme wanda꞉hali paeyaota꞉ pututuma꞉ homememe.
Mo potopede hali yaapo pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ oli ya nane pi ho̱la̱꞉make tiekema꞉ alota꞉ Do pate ipupe lea꞉me. Kutupa ipilika꞉ a꞉nda꞉ tunkiliki wanda꞉halima꞉ handa꞉pa꞉lia haena꞉ mo hali yaapota꞉ koa piti oli ya pa꞉ta꞉ pepeme.
Koto koneta꞉ yumomeni tieke pea mo daonita꞉ kiki yaapo tekili pea homeke ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ hoeyao mo daoseni watake hata꞉ wanda꞉hali homememe. Kutupa mo pa haleme wanda꞉halima꞉ta꞉ moeki handolo hata꞉ pututuma꞉ homolo oli hepeni hala꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ aneke ekina꞉ biki mina꞉liaememe.
Yaapo peao hoeyaasa꞉ hau koto paeya꞉pate mo tepo peao hoeyaasa꞉ ekita꞉ teke pa꞉ta꞉ ipilieke.
Kutupa mo watake hata꞉ enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ bu kanake lia꞉ dina꞉ta꞉ oli hepeni nane pi ho̱la̱꞉make tieke tieke manuma꞉ alota꞉ Mo kenke handeteke halo pa꞉la꞉ honkoputa꞉ ameta꞉ nika꞉ Tekehali pita꞉ ipika꞉ ma̱leke lila꞉ hali Ketiso pa꞉ta꞉ ula꞉me. Kutupa hoto paeyao handeteke hao halieke lememe.
Kutupa mo Koda꞉na꞉ puki tikitikina꞉ ika꞉ kini seana꞉ pitimi hande halitieke homekena꞉ tonkopu you haliwekita꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ yeni pitolo alota꞉
Amba꞉ pa hao hae make ame make hale Aneke Tekehali Koda꞉o. Nakana꞉ma꞉ naka꞉ wele tieke mea ameta꞉ kini pea handeteke hale ekina꞉ keiyae aloma꞉me laa alota꞉
Mo pi na miniki haleme wanda꞉halita꞉ mineke pankelememe. Pa ekipeke Koda꞉ naka꞉ mineke pankele nateta꞉ opolo a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. Homa꞉la꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ pi yokaalu pulu peleme nate a꞉pa꞉leke loa꞉me. Kutupa make naka꞉ e pokaeya꞉ potopede haliweki pa꞉ta꞉ ika꞉ yenki seliapo halo pele aneke nate a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. Mo neke pa꞉ta꞉ yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ homu pea haleme wanda꞉hali ota꞉ paeyaona꞉ nate make loa꞉me. Do kenke hoeyaaseme wanda꞉hali hoeyaalo pa꞉la꞉ nate opolo a꞉pa꞉la꞉me laa lememe.
Oli hepeni nane hala꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ tembolota꞉ lumbia꞉me. Kutupa mo hande pi la꞉ wiekeeki wieke bokosi handoa꞉me. Kutupa ti tekele make a꞉ta꞉ a꞉ta꞉ piki tutu make tutu tiekemanu make yumomeni make ya hapeke wopu make epea꞉me.
Kutupa ta꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ pea hone mateke hau tieke oli yana꞉ opolo epea꞉me. Wanda꞉ homeke koto pa꞉ta꞉ pitia꞉me. Ipika꞉ dauta꞉ mo nate yamea꞉me. Kutupa mo kaisepota꞉ ipika꞉ anke oto pa꞉ta꞉ wia kutupa ipika꞉ you aka꞉ta꞉ kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo hombulanka꞉ pambaeya꞉me.
Ipikita꞉ teke pa꞉ta꞉ weki mulu pua꞉peke yata꞉ mo weki hoki nea꞉ ekima꞉ tanda tieke pitolo hata꞉ e̱ wi lea꞉me.
Kutupa ma꞉nda꞉ ta꞉ta꞉piki ale ma꞉nda꞉ oli ya manda opolo epea꞉me. Handeta꞉ we pupapeke popake itiki hake sima꞉ handeke ale tieke hombeleke ipika꞉ amboketa꞉ paeyao watake hata꞉ hao kutupa kiki yaapo ekeke haya꞉me. Kutupa mo ambokemanu yalaota꞉ kinina꞉ you aka꞉ pamba pamba pia꞉me.
Ipika꞉ mendekema꞉ta꞉ mo hombulanka꞉manu tepo tekilipa homeke ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ mo ya mina꞉pa꞉lao yola yopua do kenkena꞉ wekila꞉ lopaeya꞉me. Mo aleta꞉ mo wanda꞉ma꞉ weki mondu lopaeya꞉ka꞉na꞉ mea nolueke alo puki tikitiki pua haya꞉me.
Kutupa mo wanda꞉ma꞉ta꞉ hali weki mondu wia꞉me. Ipiki daeyaata꞉ do kenke paeyao ayeni dopitama꞉ handeteke halo pa꞉la꞉ wekie. Pate mo wekita꞉ pa꞉ta꞉la꞉ mea Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ kini seana꞉ hala꞉ alena꞉ mea pea꞉me.
Mo wanda꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉ma꞉ ipika꞉ amu pea wia꞉yeke hapupapeke alena꞉ pindipa pea꞉me. Koto alena꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉ daoseni homeke kutupa 260 natena꞉ handeteke halo pia꞉ alena꞉e.
Kutupa oli hepeni nane a꞉nda꞉ kini pia꞉me. Maikolo ipika꞉ enisolo ame̱le̱ mo popake itiki hake si ipika꞉ enisolo ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ pimime.
Pate Maikolo tapakema꞉ mo popake itiki hake sita꞉ bepolao ipika꞉ enisolomanu tonka꞉na꞉ hepeni na haena꞉ lememe.
Mo popake itiki hake si tieke hombeleketa꞉ tolu lopaeya꞉me. Ipikita꞉ mo hande amba꞉ kiake hayeke keto biki Sadani la꞉la꞉ alee. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo kenke wanda꞉hali paeyao makeaeyeke halie. Ipikita꞉ ipika꞉ enisolo titi ame̱le̱ oni kenkena꞉ tolu lopaeya꞉me.
Kutupa oli hepeni nane pi ho̱la̱꞉make tiekema꞉ alota꞉ Ameta꞉ niki da꞉ta꞉monoyeke Koda꞉na꞉ pa꞉ta꞉la꞉la꞉eki ta a꞉pa꞉la꞉ handa꞉e. Ameta꞉ Koda꞉ ipiki kini hata꞉ ipika꞉ weleta꞉ peneme yaasa꞉ handa꞉e. Ameta꞉ ipika꞉ ma̱leke lila꞉ Ketisoma꞉ ipika꞉ handeteke hala꞉eki peneme yao wala꞉la꞉ handa꞉e. Pa ekipeke nika꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ puki tikitikina꞉ hata꞉ peliolo da kelepolo nika꞉ kamemanu ma̱leke lia hokeeki pa꞉la꞉me lo haya꞉ halita꞉ oli hepeni mina꞉pa꞉lao tolu lopaala꞉me.
Ipikita꞉ nika꞉ kame tonuma꞉ mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ wema꞉ make mo ota꞉ ekie laa waleme ekima꞉ make bepolaya꞉me. Kutupa make ikana꞉ma꞉ ika꞉ da꞉ta꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ pina꞉ pa hoeyao homa꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ pa pulumeke laa lememe.
Koto ekina꞉ta꞉ oli hepeni make koto pa꞉ta꞉ haleme wanda꞉halio paeyao ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homa꞉pee. Pate oni dawala pita꞉ kenke yaapota꞉ paala꞉e. Pa ekipeke hande Sadanita꞉ iki pa꞉ta꞉ a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. Kutupa ipikita꞉ hosiki nate lekesiki homeke ula꞉me hone witolo hata꞉ ota꞉ hoke mineke panka꞉la꞉me.
Mo popake itiki hake si tieke hombelekema꞉ ipikita꞉ mo kenke nane tolu lopaala꞉me hone wiaata꞉ mo hande weki mondu wia꞉ wanda꞉ minuluekema꞉yeke teliolo ombu haya꞉me.
Mo wanda꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ da mo hapupapeke alena꞉ pena꞉yeketa꞉ ida tiekena꞉ popake yaapo halea꞉me. Koto pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ mo popake itiki hake sima꞉ hoeyaapa꞉na꞉ bapi tepona꞉ yunki mindiki hata꞉ kaisepona꞉ handeteke halo pia꞉ pa꞉ta꞉e.
Kutupa mo popake itiki hake sima꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ epea꞉ ikali wopuma꞉ mo wanda꞉ telia꞉ mea pena꞉ lea꞉me. Handeta꞉ mo wanda꞉ ikali naa homena꞉yeke pia꞉me.
Kutu pia꞉pate kenkema꞉ mo wanda꞉ tamba꞉ minolo hata꞉ ipika꞉ kake a̱a̱ laa mo popake itiki hake sina꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ epea꞉ ikali mea neliaya꞉me.
Kutu pia꞉ ekina꞉ mo popake itiki hake si tieke hombelekema꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ mineke tieke pankolo hata꞉ ipika꞉ wekiwandiki ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ pulu pea꞉me. Koto tapaketa꞉ mo Koda꞉na꞉ pi ula꞉ ekimanu opua Yesuma꞉ peneme yaasa꞉ ota꞉eki pa꞉ta꞉ kima꞉ na homeke hone tu laeme wanda꞉halie.
Kutupa mo popake itiki hake sita꞉ dawala houna꞉ tiao haya꞉me.
Kutupa mo sayale hombeleketa꞉ mo dawala pa꞉ta꞉ pita opolo epea꞉eki handoa꞉me. Mo aleta꞉ ekeke kiki yaapo hao amboke watake hata꞉ haya꞉me. Mo ekekemanu yalaota꞉ kini you aka꞉ pambama꞉ pambama꞉ pia꞉me. Kutupa mo amboke manuna꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉ kitaake biki laememe.
Mo sayale hombeleketa꞉ bosikasi tieke ma꞉nda꞉ ipika꞉ biki lepadima꞉ handaa ipika꞉ anketa꞉ peioloma꞉ handeke ale tieke hombelekena꞉ ankema꞉ handaa ipika꞉ kaketa꞉ laeonona꞉ kakema꞉ handea꞉me. Mo hande popake itiki hake si tiekema꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ honkopu make ipika꞉ kini sea make ipika꞉ handeteke hala꞉eki tieke paeyao mo sayale hombeleke pa꞉ta꞉ halea꞉me.
Mo sayalena꞉ amboke ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ homena꞉ tupa꞉ apa꞉la꞉ pokeekepate pa mea epeayeke handaa mo wanda꞉hali paeyaota꞉ penkili putia pominolo hata꞉ mo sayale hombeleke telia꞉ mea pememe.
Kutupa wanda꞉hali paeyaoma꞉ mo popake itiki hake si pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pimime. Pa ekipeke mo sima꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ honkopu tieketa꞉ mo sayale pa꞉ta꞉ haleeke handa loa꞉me. Ikana꞉ma꞉ sayale pa꞉ta꞉ make panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pitolo alota꞉ Epita꞉ mo sayalema꞉ handelemepe. Epima꞉ ipiki ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ puluekema꞉ honkopu aneke hala꞉pe lememe.
Mo sayalema꞉ta꞉ kaisepo hali tieke yaapona꞉ pa hali ma꞉nda꞉na꞉ yaapona꞉ handeteke haena꞉ laata꞉ hakoko lita꞉la꞉eki manuma꞉ Koda꞉ kitaena꞉yeke waleke halea꞉me.
Mo sayalema꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉ make ipika꞉ biki make ipiki hala꞉ da make oli hepeni haleme wanda꞉hali paeyao make yaala꞉ma꞉ homao hoeyaasa꞉ pi kini pea lea꞉me.
Kutupa ipikana꞉ma꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉hali ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ pea bepolaena꞉ make tapake ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ make kapomani ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ handeteke hala꞉ wanda꞉hali make pi ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ make tutu ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ make paeyao handeteke haena꞉ waleke halea꞉me.
Do kenkena꞉ hala꞉ wanda꞉hali paeyaoma꞉ta꞉ mo sayale pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pilimikie. Pate do kenke a̱i̱ na wepiki haena꞉ kone ika꞉ biki manuta꞉ mo deto hala꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ biki ula꞉ bukana꞉ laala꞉ wanda꞉hali homeke homekema꞉ kotoeki na pilimikie. Koto biki ula꞉ bukata꞉ hande limiki Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ bukae.
Haleke haemeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ opua꞉pa꞉peke ya꞉la꞉me.
Ma꞉nda꞉ epita꞉ tapake ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ minina꞉e laa wia꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ota꞉ minina꞉ lelieke. Epita꞉ bainasima꞉ lia homaena꞉e laa wia꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ota꞉ mo bainasima꞉ lia homaena꞉ lelieke. Dupiki haumanu pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉hali lopaama꞉na꞉yeke homu pea pa pina꞉e laa yu wia hata꞉ make kima꞉ na homeke hone tu lao haya꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ ana꞉ pilieke.
Koto hoki naneta꞉ mo sayale hombeleke ma꞉nda꞉ mo kenke pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ opa꞉liaeyeke handoa꞉me. Do sayaleta꞉ sipisipi ma꞉na꞉ ekekema꞉ handeke ekeke yaapo haya꞉me. Kutupa ipika꞉ pita꞉ mo popake itiki hake sima꞉ ala꞉ tupa꞉ lea꞉me.
Mo alema꞉ta꞉ mo titina꞉ sayalena꞉ handeteke hala꞉eki tieke meata꞉ ipika꞉ leke popelekena꞉ hata꞉ e wopu pokea꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ do kenke make do kenkena꞉ haleme wanda꞉hali paeyao make mo amba꞉ hande titina꞉ amboke hoeyaeya꞉pate paa epea꞉ sayale pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pipee laa honkopu wopu hao sutiaeya꞉me.
Mo yaapo peao sayalema꞉ta꞉ na handeke haumanu wopu pitolo hata꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ leke popelekena꞉ oli ya nanema꞉ ti uleke do kenkena꞉ lopena꞉ lea꞉me.
Kutupa ipikana꞉ma꞉ mo titina꞉ sayalena꞉ hau peaaso hata꞉ ipika꞉ leke popelekena꞉ hata꞉ mokoto na handeke haumanu pia꞉eki manuma꞉ta꞉ do kenke wanda꞉hali paeyao makeaaso hata꞉ yola꞉ mea pea꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ wanda꞉halima꞉ mo hande bainasima꞉ hoeyaeya꞉pate pa tiao hala꞉ titina꞉ sayale yeiya꞉ laaluekema꞉ koto ekima꞉ handekeeki ma꞉nda꞉ wepia꞉pe lea꞉me.
Kutupa mo yaapo peao sayalema꞉ta꞉ mo hande titina꞉ sayale manda꞉ meao wepimi ale pa꞉ta꞉ da꞉taasa꞉ pomo halena꞉yeke waleke halea꞉me. Kutupiki hauta꞉ mo alema꞉ pi lena꞉ la make mo ipiki pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ lapeke kiaalimi wanda꞉hali paeyao lu homaena꞉yeke pia꞉me.
Mo yaapo peao sayalema꞉ta꞉ mo hosiki wanda꞉hali make aneke wanda꞉hali make hamoko wanda꞉hali make natehali wanda꞉hali make pa hameke e poka꞉la꞉ wanda꞉hali make pa haleme wanda꞉hali make paeyaoma꞉ ika꞉ popeke nane kikina꞉ o ika꞉ wenokona꞉ta꞉ maka ma꞉nda꞉ ta̱laena꞉yeke honkopu hao sutiaeya꞉me.
Kutupa ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ do maka na ta̱laeyeketa꞉ kota꞉ koto someta꞉ aleta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉manu ota꞉ na hambo make tapao pina꞉e lea꞉me. Koto makata꞉ mo sayalena꞉ biki tapa꞉ wiao o ipika꞉ bikina꞉ namba haleke ekie.
Do ekimanu opolo epea꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ epeke hone u lenkene pita꞉la꞉ somema꞉ ana꞉ pilieke. Ma꞉nda꞉ epita꞉ epeke honema꞉ tumba wia꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ipikana꞉ma꞉ koto sayalena꞉ namba lo yokena꞉e. Pa ekipeke mo nambata꞉ halina꞉ bikina꞉ anketeke minolo kone la꞉la꞉me. Koto nambata꞉ 666 la꞉la꞉me.
Kutupaka꞉na꞉ handoa꞉pate mo hande Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikita꞉ mo ipika꞉ biki make ipika꞉ Apa꞉na꞉ biki ika꞉ wenokona꞉ laemeke 144 daoseni wanda꞉hali ame̱le̱ mo Saioni potena꞉ haememe.
Kutupa oli ya nanema꞉ ikali do̱u̱ tiekema꞉ handa make tutu tieke liki nonopiki pi ho̱la̱꞉make opua꞉me. Mo pi ho̱la̱꞉maketa꞉ kidama꞉ handeke ale lita꞉la꞉ haliwekima꞉ liki nonopiki ala꞉ ekima꞉ handeke nono pia꞉me.
Mo 144 daoseni wanda꞉halita꞉ mo hande Koda꞉na꞉ kini seana꞉ make mo deto hala꞉ tonkopu ale manuna꞉ make mo you haliwekina꞉ puki tikitiki pua haememe. Ikita꞉ panake emeli ikana꞉ma꞉ homeke moka꞉la hande hande pea lapeke emeli homeke lememe. Kenke wanda꞉hali paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ koto tapake homeke pa꞉ta꞉la꞉ mea epeaalo pia꞉ tapakee.
Ikita꞉ wanda꞉weki hakopu na tunkulimieki yaalo yakopiki haliweki haememe. Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki pea꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ telipaleke ombu haememe. Ikita꞉ kenke wanda꞉hali paeyao anka꞉lopuna꞉ epeaala꞉ tapakee. Ikita꞉ Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ make mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki pa꞉ta꞉ make titina꞉ halo pa꞉la꞉ tapakee.
Ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ ikita꞉ yayapiki pi lelemeeki na opua make ala꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ ata꞉ka꞉ na pealeme haliwekie.
Kutupa enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ oli ya manda a̱e̱nolo hata꞉ do kenke wanda꞉hali paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ mo pa u hala꞉ Pi Seliapo laluekema꞉ pia꞉me. Mo wanda꞉halita꞉ tutu ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ make tapake ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ make kapomani eleke elekema꞉ handeteke hala꞉ kenke make paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ loluekema꞉ pieke handoa꞉me.
Ipikana꞉ma꞉ anekema꞉ alota꞉ Koda꞉ paala꞉ma꞉ homaaso hata꞉ ipika꞉ tieke hala꞉ ekina꞉ biki mina꞉liape. Pa ekipeke ipikana꞉ma꞉ mo hande wanda꞉hali pi yokaalu pulu pa꞉la꞉ nate a꞉pa꞉leke loa꞉me. Do kenke make oli ya make dawala make opa꞉la꞉ ikalimanu make koto ale paeyao wa꞉pa꞉la꞉ Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pea꞉pa꞉peke lea꞉me.
Kotoeki hoki naneta꞉ enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ teliolo alota꞉ Mo wanda꞉ta꞉ lopa꞉la꞉me. Aneke Ba꞉bilonita꞉ lopa꞉la꞉me. Mo wanda꞉ma꞉ wanda꞉hali paeyao ipika꞉ waini ikali nena꞉ lea꞉me. Mo honkopu hake waini ikalita꞉ ipika꞉ lokena꞉ hoke hone pa꞉la꞉eki manue lea꞉me.
Pa tepo peao enisoloma꞉ mo titina꞉eki yaapo teliolo hata꞉ anekema꞉ alota꞉ Ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ mo sayale hombeleke make koto ale manda꞉ meao wa꞉pa꞉la꞉ ale pa꞉ta꞉ make panda꞉puniao yeni pitolo o ipika꞉ maka wenoko o popeke nane kikina꞉ ta̱lena꞉ lemeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉
koto someta꞉ ipika꞉ kone Koda꞉na꞉ waini ikali nelieke. Kota꞉ mo Koda꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ paala꞉piki mineke panka꞉la꞉ wele pa ula꞉ waini ikalita꞉ mo ipika꞉ mineke panka꞉la꞉ kapo pa꞉ta꞉ holo pambeekeeki loa꞉me. Dupilia꞉ wanda꞉hali paeyaota꞉ mo yakopiki enisolo titi make mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ leke tomona꞉ mo ti uleke make mo titipu tiekepiki lanka꞉ma꞉ handeke ale pa꞉ta꞉ tanda no halimikie.
Mo tanda halo hala꞉ tina꞉ lumuta꞉ na paeyeke hoto paeyao pa u halieke. Koto sayale hombeleke pita꞉ ipika꞉ manda꞉ meao wa꞉pa꞉la꞉ ale yaapo pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeni pitolo make o koto alena꞉ bikina꞉ maka wina꞉ lea꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ koto wanda꞉hali ika꞉ tanda no halo pa꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ nate o timba꞉ ota꞉ hosiki siki na paeyaalieke lea꞉me.
Koto ya꞉leke handaa mo Koda꞉na꞉ pi ula꞉ ekimanu opua Yesu pa꞉ta꞉ kima꞉ na homeke hone tulao hala꞉ wanda꞉hali lopaama꞉na꞉yeke ika꞉ pa pina꞉e laa yu wia hala꞉ ekita꞉ ana꞉na꞉ pilieke.
Kutupa oli hepeni nanema꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉makema꞉ alota꞉ Doeki laaniae. Ame do kini pea mo Tekehalina꞉ e pokolo hata꞉ homeleme wanda꞉halita꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homa꞉pa꞉peke ya꞉la꞉me lea꞉me. Koto leeke mo Sipitidima꞉ hombo peaaso hata꞉ alota꞉ Ota꞉e. Ikita꞉ ika꞉ ki hone na wiki honkopu hao pokelemeeki paeyaemeke handaa ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homilimikie. Pa ekipeke ika꞉ e pokeleme ekina꞉ yenkita꞉ iki ame̱le̱ pa hala꞉me lea꞉me.
Kutupa handoa꞉pate ya hapi handoa꞉me. Kutupa mo ya hapi mandaata꞉ halima꞉ handeke ale pitia꞉me. Ipika꞉ ambokena꞉ta꞉ koloma꞉ wepiki kinina꞉ you aka꞉ pambao kutupa widi tunkula꞉la꞉ ne wopu hake kaiya minia꞉me.
Kutupa mo enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ mo tembolo pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ a꞉pa mo ya hapi manda pitia꞉ some pa꞉ta꞉ e̱ wi tieke la꞉moneaaso alota꞉ Naka꞉ widi tunkulu hale kaiyama꞉ ne napeke mie. Pa ekipeke mo nateta꞉ a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. Kutupa kenkena꞉ ne napeke mina꞉ pota꞉leke loa꞉me lea꞉me.
Koto leeke mo ya hapi manda pitia꞉ somema꞉ ipika꞉ widi tunkulu hala꞉ kaiya wankeaaso hata꞉ kenkena꞉ ne napeke mu paeyaeya꞉me.
Kutupa enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ mo tembolo pa꞉ta꞉ pita opolu bao ipulu ne wopu hake kaiya ombu miniki epea꞉me.
Kutupa mo tina꞉ handeteke haya꞉ enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ mo oloda pa꞉ta꞉ hao epea꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ mo ne wopu hake kaiya miniki haya꞉ enisolo pa꞉ta꞉ anekema꞉ alota꞉ Naka꞉ kaiyama꞉ mo waini puna꞉ kilikimanu honda꞉ poka꞉e. Pa ekipeke mo kiliki manuta꞉ pota꞉leke loa꞉me lea꞉me.
Kota꞉ mo enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kaiya do kenkena꞉ wankeaaso hata꞉ mo waini kiliki manuta꞉ talo pamba oni Koda꞉na꞉ paala꞉ piki mineke panka꞉la꞉ waini kiliki dekepo hala꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ lopaeya꞉me.
Mo waini kilikita꞉ mo daoni tieke hama꞉ nane mo waini kiliki dekepo hala꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ dekepea꞉me. Kutupa mo dekepea꞉ ale pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ we ikali tieke 300 kilomida hokulu taa hata꞉ ota꞉ kendo tieke make mo hosina꞉ kake ana꞉na꞉ lombei pea꞉peke kendo wia꞉me.
Kutupa oli yana꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ piki hone mateke pututu au tieke handoa꞉me. Watake hata꞉ enisolo manuma꞉ paeyaaso ane mone ke handaasa꞉ ipula꞉ watake hata꞉ haumanu miniki haememe. Kotota꞉ Koda꞉ ipika꞉ paeyaaso mineke panka꞉la꞉eki walo paeyaasa꞉eki yekeme.
Kutupa mo kalasima꞉ handeke hama꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ ti uleke apa꞉taakeeki handoa꞉me. Koto pa꞉ta꞉ make mo hande sayale hombeleke make koto ale manda꞉ meao wepimiki sayale make mo alena꞉ bikina꞉ taapa꞉ wiao la꞉la꞉ namba make bepolao haleme wanda꞉hali handoa꞉me. Ikita꞉ mo kalasi hama꞉ tea꞉na꞉ tilao hata꞉ Koda꞉ma꞉ hala꞉la꞉ kidama꞉ handeke alemanu miniki hata꞉
mo Koda꞉na꞉ e pokeeke hali Mosesina꞉ emeli make mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ emeli make lememe. Ikana꞉ma꞉ alota꞉ Aneke Tekehali Koda꞉o. Naka꞉ pita꞉la꞉eki manuta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ peao make yole make pa꞉la꞉me. Tapake paeyaona꞉ kinio. Naka꞉ pitele haumanu paeyaota꞉ tikitiki pea ota꞉ hau manue.
Tekehali neketa꞉ epima꞉ paala꞉ma꞉ na homilia꞉pe. Naka꞉ hau tieke laaluekema꞉ta꞉ epima꞉ kiaalia꞉pe. Neke homeke homeke yako peleme. Wanda꞉hali paeyaota꞉ neke pa꞉ta꞉ a꞉pa panda꞉ puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pilimikie. Pa ekipeke naka꞉ yakopiki hau manuta꞉ paeyaoma꞉ amba꞉ handelememe lememe.
Koto hoki naneta꞉ oli hepeni nane mo tembolo da pota꞉ lumba wiekeeki handoa꞉me. Kutupa mo da tukikina꞉ta꞉ amba꞉ hande Koda꞉ ipika꞉ wanda꞉hali ame̱le̱ pi lo hayeke palai da handoa꞉me.
Mo watake hata꞉ enisolo manuta꞉ mo watake hata꞉ ke handa꞉peke ekimanu miniki hata꞉ tembolo pa꞉ta꞉ hao epememe. Ikita꞉ hake piki leke yale yale piki dau yama koloma꞉ wepiki beleke ika꞉ hakokona꞉ yamemekeme.
Kutupa mo hande deto hala꞉ tonkopu ale homekema꞉ mo watake hata꞉ enisolomanu pa꞉ta꞉ mo hoto paeyao pa hao halo pa꞉la꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ mineke panka꞉la꞉ ekima꞉ tumbiki watake hata꞉ kawasomanu halea꞉me.
Mo Koda꞉na꞉ wele pita꞉ pa̱a̱ yaapo pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ epea꞉ lumuma꞉ta꞉ mo tembolo tumbulu baeya꞉me. Kutupa mo tembolo pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ pua꞉peke na ya꞉pate pa mo watake hata꞉ enisolo manuma꞉ mo watake hata꞉ ke handaasa꞉eki mea ipu paeya꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ wetepena꞉ pua꞉peke ya꞉me.
Kutupa mo tembolo pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉make wopuma꞉ mo watake hata꞉ enisolo pa꞉ta꞉ alota꞉ Kenkena꞉ pua mo Koda꞉na꞉ mineke panka꞉la꞉eki pamba꞉la꞉ watake hata꞉ kawasomanu hola꞉pe lea꞉me.
Koto ekina꞉ titina꞉ enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawaso kenkena꞉ pua holaeya꞉me. Kutu pieke handaa ota꞉ hoke tanda tieke piki boleke manuta꞉ mo hande hoke sayalena꞉ maka talaeme tapake make mo ale manda꞉ meao wepimiki ale pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeni pu haeme wanda꞉hali pa꞉ta꞉ pua pitia꞉me.
Kutupa yaapo peao enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawaso mo dawala manda pua holaeya꞉me. Mo ikalita꞉ homeke halina꞉ wema꞉ handaata꞉ koto dawala pa꞉ta꞉ pitimi ale paeyao homememe.
Kutupa tepo peao enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawaso mea pua mo ikalimanu make opa꞉la꞉ ikali pa꞉ta꞉manu holaeya꞉ dina꞉ta꞉ we au lolo yapea꞉me.
Kutupa mo ikalimanu handeteke haya꞉ enisoloma꞉ alota꞉ Naka꞉ panisi pealuekema꞉ ma̱leke liaasa꞉eki manuta꞉ ota꞉ ana꞉na꞉ kone wa꞉peleme. O ota꞉ yako piki someo. Neke ame hale make amba꞉ hae makee.
Pa ekipeke ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ we make mo potopede haliwekina꞉ we make holememe. Koto ekina꞉ ame nakana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ iki make we ikali nena꞉ haleleme. Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ika꞉ ekina꞉ yenki kone mina꞉lememe laa lea꞉me.
Kutupa mo oloda pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉makema꞉ alota꞉ Wele wopupiki Tekehali Koda꞉o. Naka꞉ panisi pealuekema꞉ ma̱leke liaasa꞉eki manuta꞉ tikitiki pea make ota꞉ ana꞉na꞉ wepeleme lea꞉me.
Koto hoki naneta꞉ mo tonko peao enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawasota꞉ natena꞉ holaeya꞉me. Kutupa mo nate ipika꞉ wele wopu piki titipuma꞉ wanda꞉hali tena꞉ waleke halea꞉me.
Mo wanda꞉halita꞉ do wele wopupiki titipuma꞉ to tokilieke handaata꞉ mo ke manuna꞉ handeteke haya꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ biki hoeyaememe. Kutu pimipate ika꞉ hoke hau manuta꞉ hoki na walaa ipika꞉ wele tiekena꞉ biki na mea mina꞉liaememe.
Kutupa mo yunki peao enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawasota꞉ mo hoke sayalena꞉ kini seana꞉ pua holaeya꞉me. Kutu pieke handaa timba꞉ ala꞉ ekima꞉ mo hande sayalena꞉ kilu tombuao hala꞉ alena꞉ tumbaeya꞉me. Kutupa wanda꞉halima꞉ tanda tieke nalo hata꞉ ika꞉ kekeke tankolo nememe.
Kutu pitolo hata꞉ ika꞉ tanda make tete manuna꞉ oli hepeni hala꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ biki hoeyaemepate ika꞉ hoke hau manuta꞉ hoki na walememe.
Kutupa mo yunki mindiki peao enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawasota꞉ mo ikali tieke biki Yupoteitisina꞉ holaeya꞉me. Kutupa mo nate opa꞉la꞉ nane haleme kini manuna꞉ pota꞉ wiaaso mo hande ikalita꞉ hapupa pea꞉me.
Kutupa ki̱ma꞉ handeke ha̱i̱ pambeke temoko tepo handoa꞉me. Ikita꞉ mo popake itiki hake sina꞉ handeke alena꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ make mo hoke sayale hombelekena꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ make mo yayapiki potopedena꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ make pita꞉ opolu bao epememe.
Ikita꞉ mo na handeke haumanu pu haleme hoke temokomanue. Mo hoke temoko tepoma꞉ta꞉ do kenke honiki paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ hala꞉ kinimanu pua hatuku mea a꞉pa mo Wele Wopupiki Koda꞉na꞉ Aneke natena꞉ a꞉nda꞉ pina꞉ yeke pimikime.
Opie. I̱ta꞉ pake nala꞉ hali leke ipulueke. U̱ na peliki hata꞉ ipika꞉ aka꞉manu wopu handeteke hao hale someta꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homilieke. Ipikita꞉ paa tia pominolo hata꞉ wanda꞉hali leke popelekena꞉ yaala꞉ meaapa꞉na꞉yeke pita꞉la꞉me.
Kutupa mo hande temoko tepoma꞉ mo kinimanu hatuku a꞉pa mo Hibulu pima꞉ta꞉ Amakedoni la꞉la꞉ alena꞉ a꞉pa momba꞉laeya꞉me.
Kutupa mo watake peao enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ kawasota꞉ oli ya pa꞉ta꞉ holaeya꞉me. Oni mo tembolo pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ aneke pi ho̱la̱꞉make alota꞉ Ameta꞉ koto paela꞉ handa꞉e lea꞉me.
Kutupa ti tekelemanu make a꞉ta꞉ a꞉ta꞉ piki tutumanu make tutu tiekemanu make ota꞉ hoke yu momeni make pia꞉me. Amba꞉ hali wepia kini pea a꞉pa ame do make kutupiki yu momeni na pa꞉la꞉pate do yu momeni homeketa꞉ paeyao ankulake ota꞉ hoke ta꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ pikieki ya꞉mee.
Mo aneke daonita꞉ tepo tekilipa mo kenke paeyaona꞉ daoni paeyaota꞉ ota꞉ hoeyaeya꞉me. Koda꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo hande Ba꞉biloni tieketa꞉ pa niminaaso hata꞉ ipika꞉ wopu mineke panka꞉la꞉ waini ikali ipika꞉ kapona꞉ nena꞉ lea꞉me.
Mo dawalama꞉ dupala꞉ kenkemanu paeyaota꞉ alu pao mo potemanu paeyaota꞉ alupaeya꞉me.
Leke opeke ya hapeke tieke tiekemanu ka꞉nda꞉ ota꞉ tieke hombeleke piki ekimanu oli ya nanema꞉ yama꞉ a꞉pa wanda꞉hali manda lopea꞉me. Koto wanda꞉halima꞉ta꞉ mo ke handaeya꞉ ya hapekena꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ biki hoeyaememe. Pa ekipeke do keta꞉ ota꞉ hokeeki ya꞉mee.
Kutupa mo hande watake hata꞉ kawaso miniki haeme watake hata꞉ enisolo homeke ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ a꞉pa alota꞉ Epoe. I̱ma꞉ mo hali yolo hala꞉ biki wiki wanda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ halo pa꞉la꞉ panisi walueke. Mo ikalimanu tea꞉na꞉ a꞉ela꞉ aneke daoni hombelekema꞉ loa꞉me.
Do kenkena꞉ hala꞉ kini manuma꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉ ame̱le̱ hoke loke hoeyaasa꞉ hau pu ombu haememe. Kutupa mo kenke wanda꞉halima꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ loke hoeyaasa꞉ hau manuna꞉ waini ikali naa keaememe lea꞉me.
Mo Sipitidima꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ e pokolo hata꞉ mo enisoloma꞉ I̱ta꞉ hapu hala꞉ alena꞉ mea tia pea꞉me. Koto pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ wanda꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ mo wepiki sayale ma꞉nda꞉na꞉ hoki manda pitia꞉eki handoa꞉me. Mo sayalena꞉ loke paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉ kitaasa꞉ bikimanu lao kutupa ipikita꞉ watake hata꞉ amboke hao make kiki yaapo ekekemanu haya꞉me.
Mo wanda꞉ ipika꞉ aka꞉ta꞉ we ta꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ yaapo piki au lekeeki yamea꞉me. Kutupa mo aka꞉ta꞉ koloma꞉ wepiki beleke manuma꞉ make seliapo piki toopi manuma꞉ make sekete inkiki manuma꞉ make tumbulu baeya꞉me. Ipika꞉ kiki pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ loke hoeyaasa꞉ ekina꞉ yenkita꞉ ota꞉ yaala꞉piki ekimanu make ha̱i̱ pambeke alemanu make tumbulu baeyeke koloma꞉ wepiki kapo miniki haya꞉me.
Mo ipika꞉ wenokona꞉ta꞉ hande a꞉mbaala꞉ ekina꞉ biki dupa wiekeme. Hali yola꞉la꞉ wanda꞉hali make kikana꞉ haumanu pu haleme wanda꞉hali make iki paeyaona꞉ inkiki Ba꞉biloni tieke laa wia꞉me.
Kutupa mo wanda꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ make Yesu pa꞉ta꞉ hone tulaa pelia haemeke handa limiki wanda꞉halina꞉ we na̱a̱ keaya꞉eki handoa꞉me. I̱ma꞉ moeki hando haota꞉ ota꞉ hoke tupa꞉ penkilipa꞉tia pomua꞉me.
Mo enisoloma꞉ I̱ lota꞉ pitolo alota꞉ Neketa꞉ ekipeke penkilipa꞉tia pominelepe. I̱ma꞉ neke pa꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉na꞉ make mo wanda꞉ mea tia pomu hala꞉ sayalena꞉ a꞉mbao ula꞉ ekina꞉ teke la kionoe. Mo hande watake hata꞉ amboke hao make kiki yaapo ekeke hala꞉ sayalena꞉ loa꞉me.
Koto sayaleta꞉ amba꞉ta꞉ da꞉ta haya꞉pate ameta꞉ na da꞉taa hala꞉me. Ipikita꞉ ame do siki mo honiki na wiki naku kiake pa꞉ta꞉ hama opolu bao ipiki hoeyaena꞉ pelieke. Do kenkena꞉ haleme wanda꞉hali ika꞉ biki manuta꞉ do kenke a̱i̱ na wepiki haena꞉ kone mo deto hala꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ biki ula꞉ bukana꞉ ika꞉ biki na lake wanda꞉halita꞉ mo hande sayale handolo hata꞉ penkilipa꞉tia pomilimikie. Amba꞉ a꞉nda꞉ta꞉ da꞉ta haya꞉pate ameta꞉ na deteke hala꞉me. Pate paa opolo ipilieke.
Doeki manuta꞉ hone u lenkene pita꞉la꞉eki pita꞉ hone wita꞉la꞉eki yaapoma꞉ handa꞉peke ya꞉la꞉ haue. Mo watake hata꞉ amboketa꞉ watake hata꞉ yueli manue. Kotota꞉ mo hande wanda꞉ pila꞉ alena꞉e. Kutupa make ikita꞉ watake hata꞉ kini manue.
Yunki hata꞉ta꞉ lopelemepate homekema꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ kilu tombuao hala꞉ ekina꞉ pa handeteke hala꞉me. Kutupa ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ a̱i̱ na a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. Ipiki epea꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ nate hosiki sikima꞉ homeke handeteke halieke.
Kutupa mo hande amba꞉ta꞉ da꞉ta haya꞉pate ame na da꞉ta hala꞉ sayaleta꞉ ipika꞉ kone ketepo peao kinie. Mo hande watake hata꞉ tapake konee. Ipikita꞉ hoeyaena꞉ pula꞉me.
Mo hande kiki yaapo ekeke manuta꞉ kiki yaapo kini manue. Ikita꞉ a̱i̱ na kini pea handeteke halemepate pa aowa homeke homekena꞉ mo hoke sayale ame̱le̱ handeteke haena꞉ waleke halieke.
Do kiki yaapo ale ikita꞉ teke homeke homeke wia halememe. Ika꞉ honkopu make ika꞉ handeteke haleme wele manuta꞉ mo sayale pa꞉ta꞉ halelememe.
Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ pilimikie. Pate mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikita꞉ ipika꞉ wi laa yata꞉pa꞉ ma꞉la꞉ hone tulao haleme hoki nane tolu haleme tapake ame̱le̱ hata꞉ mo tapake bepolalimikie. Pa ekipeke ipikita꞉ tekehali paeyaona꞉ Tekehali make kini paeyaona꞉ Kinie lea꞉me.
Mo enisoloma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ ombu alota꞉ Mo hande hande hali yolo hala꞉ wanda꞉ pitia꞉ ikali manuta꞉ kapomani ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ handeteke hala꞉ kenkemanu make mo ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ piki wanda꞉hali paeyao make mo tutu ta꞉ta꞉manu make pi ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ leke tapake manue.
Mo hande hande kiki yaapo ekeke manuma꞉ make mo hande sayalema꞉ make ikana꞉ma꞉ mo wanda꞉ ota꞉ honditi pilimikie. Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉ma꞉ pambala꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ paeyao hola꞉ mea pa tia haena꞉ lelimikie. Mo wanda꞉na꞉ loke mindiki naa kutupa ti ulekema꞉ hoeyaalimikie.
Pa ekipeke Koda꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ hone pa꞉la꞉eki peaena꞉ yeke ika꞉ puki pa꞉ta꞉manu ipika꞉ hone pa꞉la꞉eki wina꞉ leeke handaa ikana꞉ma꞉ ta꞉ma꞉ni pea homeke tupa꞉ hau pilimikie. Ika꞉ honkoputa꞉ mo sayale pa꞉ta꞉ halaata꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ pimanu ota꞉ peneme yaalo epena꞉ lelimikie.
Mo hande wanda꞉ta꞉ mo aneke daoni hombelekee. Mo kenke honiki paeyaona꞉ kinimanu handeteke hala꞉ daonie laa lea꞉me.
Doeki hoki naneta꞉ enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ oli hepeni nane hao hola꞉pa꞉nialo epea꞉eki handoa꞉me. Ipikita꞉ wele tieke pa꞉ta꞉ ipulu ipika꞉ yameeke leke yale yale piki pa̱a̱ma꞉ta꞉ do kenke paeyao pa̱a̱ peaya꞉me.
Ipikana꞉ma꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉make tiekema꞉ e̱ wi alo alota꞉ Mo wanda꞉ta꞉ lopa꞉la꞉me. Ba꞉biloni tieketa꞉ lopa꞉la꞉me. Ipikita꞉ hoke temoko tonuma꞉ make ha̱i̱ pambeke temokomanu haleme teke dae. Ota꞉ ha̱i̱ pamba꞉papeke make handa꞉ nala꞉ na piki anemone ba manuta꞉ koto pa꞉ta꞉ pila꞉me.
Pa ekipeke mo kapomani ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ma꞉ handeteke hala꞉ tapake paeyaoma꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ waini ikali nememe. Mo honkopu wopu hake waini ikali ipika꞉ loke hoeyaasa꞉ na꞉na꞉ pa꞉la꞉ hauna꞉ loa꞉me. Do kenkena꞉ kini manuma꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉ ame̱le̱ loke hoeyaasa꞉ hau pu ombu haememe. Kutupa do kenkena꞉ bisinisi haliwekita꞉ mo wanda꞉na꞉ kikana꞉ hau leke pia꞉ hoke hau pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ hamoko haememe lea꞉me.
Kutupa I̱ma꞉ opua꞉pate oli hepeni nanema꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉make ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ alota꞉ Ya wanda꞉halio. Opolu bao ipupee. Koto wanda꞉ mina꞉pa꞉lao ipupee. Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ hoke haumanu pa꞉ta꞉ na apa꞉taapa꞉pee. Ipika꞉ hoke yenki mina꞉la꞉eki na telipa mia꞉pa꞉pee.
Pa ekipeke ipika꞉ hoke hau manuta꞉ oli hepeni wataalo a꞉ma꞉ela꞉me. Kutupa Koda꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ hoke hau pa꞉la꞉ ekimanu hone niminaasa꞉me.
Iki pa꞉ta꞉ pia꞉ tupa꞉ ipiki pa꞉ta꞉ make homeke tupa꞉ pipee. Ipika꞉ pia꞉ ekina꞉ hoke yenkita꞉ pa atulao hala꞉pe. Ikana꞉ma꞉ hokeeki nomena꞉yeke ipikana꞉ma꞉ amu peawaya꞉ tupa꞉ ikana꞉ma꞉ make ipika꞉ kapo pa꞉ta꞉ mo yaapo peao honkopu wopu hake ikali tumbape.
Ipika꞉ kone mo pa̱a̱ pa꞉la꞉eki make ta꞉na꞉ tieke pa꞉la꞉eki make halolo pia꞉ tupa꞉ kone paa mo tanda tiekemanu make homena꞉ tupa꞉ tanda mina꞉la꞉eki make hala꞉pe. Pa ekipeke ipika꞉ kone alota꞉ Kini wanda꞉ do pilu handa꞉e. I̱ta꞉ kineke wanda꞉ dia꞉me. I̱ma꞉ta꞉ hamono tupa꞉ tanda mina꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ ota꞉ na handulueke laa ala꞉me.
Do ekina꞉ yeketa꞉ nate ma꞉nda꞉na꞉ ipikita꞉ ke eleke elekema꞉ minilieke. Do ke manuta꞉ yeni ki make homena꞉ tupa꞉ tanda mina꞉la꞉eki make tea꞉ ki makee. Kutupa ipikita꞉ ti ulekema꞉ yankilieke. Pa ekipeke mo wanda꞉ panisi peaasa꞉ Tekehali Koda꞉ta꞉ ota꞉ wele wopu pa꞉la꞉me.
Do kenkena꞉ haleme kinimanu mo wanda꞉ ame̱le̱ loke apa꞉tao hoke na꞉na꞉ pa꞉la꞉ haumanu mandakena꞉ pimi tapakema꞉ta꞉ mo daoni tiekena꞉ e̱ lelimikie. Mo yanko paeyaasa꞉ ti ulekena꞉ lumu handolo hata꞉ loa꞉me.
Ikita꞉ mo wanda꞉na꞉ mina꞉la꞉ tandata꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ putupa mea꞉peke yeke paala꞉ma꞉ homolo hata꞉ ota꞉ papate leke halememe. Ikana꞉ma꞉ alota꞉ A꞉pa꞉e. Ota꞉ paala꞉e. Do aneke make honkopu hake daoni Ba꞉bilonio. Nate leke homeke sikina꞉ kone neketa꞉ panisi ka꞉la꞉me laa lelimikie.
Do kenkena꞉ bisinisi haliwekima꞉ make mo wanda꞉na꞉ e̱ alo make a꞉ta꞉ma꞉ make homelememe. Pa ekipeke ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ ika꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ ota꞉ na hambelememe.
Ika꞉ kolo make silipa make seliapo piki toopimanu make sekete inkikimanu make dau panka꞉manu make ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ piki wepiki daumanu make silika daumanu make mandane ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ piki wopu na hala꞉ timanu make elepa꞉ntina꞉ ekekema꞉ wa꞉pele ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ piki alemanu make yenki tieke wiki timanu make kopama꞉ handeke ale botonosi make ayenima꞉ wepiki alemanu make kalasima꞉ handeke hakesapo biki mambolo
make mandane ti manuna꞉ yonkeleke make teika꞉ma꞉ handeke ale make totopo yole piki ale make hosiki tima꞉ handeke maetamo leke ti make totopo wopu piki oeta make waini ikali make pa oeta make palaowa make widi make kao make sipisipi make hosi make hosi ma꞉na꞉ma꞉ yolaa pula꞉ da꞉ta꞉ka mendeke make e pa hameke pokaaseme haliweki make halina꞉ da꞉ta꞉la꞉eki kone ota꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ ame do hamba꞉peke na ya꞉me.
Mo bisinisi haliwekima꞉ mo wanda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ alota꞉ Naka꞉ ekie laa Naka꞉ hande wia hae epeke ale manuta꞉ alu pa꞉la꞉me. Kutupa naka꞉ hande hamoko hale alemanu make neke au le yole pa꞉la꞉ ale manuta꞉ paeyaota꞉ alu pa꞉la꞉me. Nakana꞉ma꞉ ota꞉ paa na handa꞉ wilipikie laa lelimikie.
Koto daoni pa꞉ta꞉ bisinisi pitolo hata꞉ hamoko haeme bisinisi haliwekita꞉ ota꞉ papate pua halimikie. Pa ekipeke mo wanda꞉na꞉ mina꞉la꞉ tanda putupa mea pekeyeke loa꞉me. Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ e̱ alo make a꞉ta꞉ma꞉ homolota꞉ do lelimikie.
Mo aneke daoni hombeleketa꞉ a꞉pa꞉e ota꞉ paala꞉e. Ipikita꞉ hakepiki aka꞉ panka꞉ma꞉ make ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ piki wepiki dauma꞉ make yama kutupa koloma꞉ wepiki beleke manuma꞉ make seliapo piki toopi manuma꞉ make sekete inkikima꞉ make dupao yama꞉tiki pu haya꞉me.
Pate nateleke homeke sikina꞉ kone do hamoko alemanu paeyao alu paeya꞉me. Mo dawalana꞉ sipi you haliweki make mo sipina꞉ pua꞉tiki pimi wanda꞉hali make mo sipina꞉ e poka꞉la꞉ haliweki make mo dawalana꞉ ane mone e pokeme wanda꞉hali paeyao make papate haememe.
Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉ mea neliaya꞉ ti ulekena꞉ lumu handolo hata꞉ e̱ wi tieke alo hata꞉ alota꞉ Dupiki aneke daoni hombeleke ma꞉nda꞉ na haya꞉me lea꞉me.
Ika꞉ ambokenina꞉ dokolo mea lopaaso hata꞉ e̱ alo make a꞉ta꞉ma꞉ homolo hata꞉ alota꞉ A꞉pa꞉e. Ota꞉ paala꞉e. Mo koto aneke daoni ota꞉ paala꞉e. Ipikita꞉ ipika꞉ hamoko hala꞉ ekima꞉ mo dawalana꞉ pomina꞉la꞉ sipi teke haliwekita꞉ hamoko haememe. Kutupa nateleke homekena꞉ kone ipika꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ paeyao alu paeya꞉me lememe.
Hepenio ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homa꞉e. Pa ekipeke ipikita꞉ hoeyaala꞉ ekina꞉ loa꞉me. Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉hali make mo aposolo haliweki make potopede haliweki make ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homa꞉pee. Pa ekipeke mo wanda꞉ma꞉ iki pa꞉ta꞉ pia꞉ ekina꞉ Koda꞉ma꞉ ipiki hoeyaala꞉me.
Kutupa wele wopu piki enisoloma꞉ mo ka꞉nda꞉ ota꞉ tieke piki toopi tieke mea oni dawala pa꞉ta꞉ yombu lopaaso hata꞉ alota꞉ Do hande aneke daoni Ba꞉bilonita꞉ dupa anekema꞉ mea lopa꞉niao ota꞉ pa na handolo pa꞉la꞉ tupa꞉e.
Mo kidama꞉ handeke alena꞉ e̱ make wanda꞉halina꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉makemanu make mo soke lu haleme wanda꞉hali make mo bu kanake make neke tukiki pa꞉ta꞉ ota꞉ na opilimikie. Kutupa mo ane mone e pokeleme haliwekita꞉ neke pa꞉ta꞉ ota꞉ na halimikie. Kutupa mo palaowa yombita꞉la꞉ ka꞉nda꞉piki toopina꞉ e̱ make ota꞉ na opilimikie.
Lamepana꞉ pa̱a̱ta꞉ neke pa꞉ta꞉ ota꞉ na handilimikie. Kutupa mo halina꞉ da panake pula꞉ wanda꞉na꞉ make wanda꞉ panake mina꞉la꞉ halina꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉make make ota꞉ na opilimikie. Naka꞉ bisinisi haliwekita꞉ kenke honiki paeyao lu tumbao honkopu wopu haeme make naka꞉ yayapiki ha̱i̱piki ti̱o̱ haumanu pi ekima꞉ta꞉ do kenke wanda꞉hali paeyao makeaememe laa lea꞉me.
Ba꞉biloni panisi peake hauta꞉ mo potopede haliweki make Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ weta꞉ mo daoni pa꞉ta꞉ wieke pia꞉me. Ota꞉e. Mo kenkena꞉ lia꞉ wanda꞉hali paeyaona꞉ we paeyao wia꞉me.
Doeki hoki naneta꞉ oli hepeni nane wanda꞉hali tiekema꞉ leke nono pea alota꞉ Haleluya. (Nika꞉ pima꞉ta꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ biki miniliamana꞉e) Da꞉ta꞉mono yeke pa꞉ta꞉la꞉la꞉eki make pa̱a̱ peaasa꞉eki make wele tieke make nika꞉ Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ ula꞉me.
Ipika꞉ pi yokaalu pita꞉la꞉eki manuta꞉ ota꞉eki make tikitiki pikieki makee. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo hande hali yolo haya꞉ wanda꞉ ipika꞉ loke hoeyaasa꞉ hauma꞉ kenke paeyao hoeyaeyeke handaa ketete peleme laa ma̱leke liaata꞉ ipikita꞉ panisi peala꞉me. Pa ekipeke mo wanda꞉ma꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ e pokaeya꞉ wanda꞉hali lu homaeyeke handaa loa꞉me laa lememe.
Paa e̱ wi alo alota꞉ Haleluya. Mo hande aneke daoni mea neliaya꞉ lumuta꞉ honiki na wiki hoto paeyao pa a꞉meiyu hala꞉me lememe.
Mo hali tieke homekena꞉ tonkopu you haliweki make mo deto haleme tonkopu ale manuma꞉ make panda꞉puniao lopa mo kini seana꞉ pitia꞉ Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pimime. Ikana꞉ma꞉ alota꞉ Kutu pina꞉e. Haleluya lememe.
Kutupa mo kini sea pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉makema꞉ alota꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ e pokaaseme tapake make ipiki yeiya꞉ laaseme wanda꞉hali make iki paeyaoma꞉ nika꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ biki miniliapee. Mo aneke wanda꞉hali pa꞉ta꞉ make natehali wanda꞉halisunu pa꞉ta꞉ make loa꞉me lea꞉me.
Kutupa e̱ ala꞉eki ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ mo wanda꞉hali hombuta꞉ hombeleke hata꞉ make ikali dou lopolo make tutu tieke litolo make leke nono pia꞉eki dupa opua꞉me. Haleluya. Mo Tekehali nika꞉ Aneke Koda꞉ta꞉ kini hala꞉me.
Koto ekina꞉ niki paeyao ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homomana꞉e. Ipika꞉ tieke hala꞉ ekina꞉ biki mea miniliamana꞉e. Pa ekipeke mo hande Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ wanda꞉ mulu pa꞉la꞉ nateta꞉ opolo a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. Ipika꞉ panake wanda꞉ta꞉ mo ekina꞉ amba꞉ tikitiki yao hala꞉me.
Mo wanda꞉ta꞉ hake pea leke yale yale piki dau yamena꞉ hala꞉la꞉me laa lememe. Koto dauta꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ epeke hau piteleme ekie.
Kutupa mo enisoloma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ alota꞉ Doeki laaniae. Mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ wanda꞉ mina꞉la꞉ ekina꞉ ne pamba꞉la꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ epoa꞉ la꞉la꞉ wanda꞉halita꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homa꞉pee. Kutupa mo enisoloma꞉ apa꞉taaso alota꞉ Dota꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ ota꞉ pimanue lea꞉me.
I̱ta꞉ ipiki yeiya꞉ lao yeni puluku alo ipika꞉ anke teke pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao lopoa꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ ipikana꞉ma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ alota꞉ Ei I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ kotoeki na pia꞉pema. I̱ta꞉ e pokaaso naka꞉ yankekee. Kutupa make naka꞉ kamemanu mo Yesuma꞉ peneme yaeya꞉ ota꞉ pimanu miniki haleme wanda꞉halina꞉ yankeke halome. Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ homeke yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pu hapeke laa lea꞉me. Pa ekipeke mo Yesuma꞉ peneme yaeya꞉ ota꞉ ekita꞉ mo potopede haliwekima꞉ alemeeki hone u tiaasa꞉ekie.
Kutupa oli hepeni lumba꞉pa wia mo hakepiki hosi ma꞉na꞉ handoa꞉me. Mo hosi hokina꞉ pitia꞉ halina꞉ bikita꞉ Kima꞉ na homeke hone tu laala꞉eki pita꞉ Ota꞉eki yaapoe lea꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ tikitiki piki hauma꞉ pi yokaalu pea make ipika꞉ a꞉nda꞉ ipula꞉eki a꞉nda꞉ pu hala꞉me.
Ipika꞉ leketa꞉ titipu pupapeke ti haleke ekima꞉ handaa ipika꞉ ambokena꞉ta꞉ kini you aka꞉ eleke eleke pambaeya꞉me. Biki ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ mo somena꞉ laeya꞉pate koto bikita꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ma꞉ hone na ula꞉pate ipika꞉ homeke hone ula꞉me.
Ipika꞉ pambaeyeke aka꞉ hokuluta꞉ wema꞉ tote pia꞉me. Ipika꞉ bikita꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ Pie.
Mo hepenina꞉ ami manuma꞉ta꞉ ipiki telia꞉ mea pememe. Ikana꞉ma꞉ hakepiki hosi manda pita꞉ hakepiki aka꞉ yamememe.
Ipika꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ do kenkena꞉ kapomani paeyaoma꞉ handeteke hala꞉ tapake lu bepolaena꞉ ne wopu hake bainasi opolu baeya꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo ayeni dopitama꞉ iki handeteke hata꞉ mo Aneke Koda꞉ paala꞉ piki mineke panka꞉la꞉ waini dekepo hala꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ pa ula꞉ waini da꞉ka꞉pa꞉ tumba bepilieke.
Ipika꞉ aka꞉ hokuluna꞉ make ipika꞉ palekena꞉ maketa꞉ biki dupa laeya꞉me. Kini paeyaona꞉ kinie laa Tekehali paeyaona꞉ Tekehalie.
Kutupa mo natena꞉ tiao haya꞉ enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ handoa꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ mo ya tukikina꞉ a̱e̱ya̱ pomimi bamanu pa꞉ta꞉ anekema꞉ wi la꞉moneaaso alota꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ aneke yawe lita꞉la꞉eki pa꞉ta꞉ a꞉pa momba꞉la꞉pee laata꞉
A꞉pa mo kini manuna꞉ make ami you haliwekina꞉ make ami titina꞉ loke make paeyao a꞉pa napee. Kutupa hosi ma꞉na꞉ manuna꞉ loke make hosi mea pomu haleme haliwekina꞉ loke make wanda꞉hali paeyao pa hameke e poka꞉la꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ loke make pa haleme wanda꞉halina꞉ loke make natehali wanda꞉halina꞉ loke make aneke wanda꞉halina꞉ loke paeyao a꞉pa napee lea꞉me.
Kutupa mo hande sayale tieke hombeleke make do kenkena꞉ kinimanu make ika꞉ ami paeyaoma꞉ mo hande hosi hokina꞉ pitia꞉ hali pita꞉ ipika꞉ ami ame̱le̱ a꞉nda꞉ puluekema꞉ mombelememe.
Mo sayale make mo sayalena꞉ leke popelekena꞉ na handeke haumanu pia꞉ makeaaso potopede hali make dipula minimime. Koto pia꞉ na handeke hau manuma꞉ta꞉ ipikana꞉ma꞉ mo sayalena꞉ tombo ika꞉ wenokona꞉ wimi wanda꞉hali make mo manda꞉ meao wepimi sayale pa꞉ta꞉ yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pimi wanda꞉hali make makeaeya꞉me. Mo sayale tieke hombeleke pita꞉ mo makeaaso potopede hali yaapo pa pitiki oni titipupiki lanka꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ solopa tala꞉ ti uleke kiake pa꞉ta꞉ lopaememe.
Ika꞉ ami titita꞉ mo hosi ma꞉na꞉ hokina꞉ pitia꞉ halina꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ epea꞉ bainasima꞉ lu petepete pia꞉me. Kutupa mo ba manuma꞉ mo tokomanu naaka꞉na꞉ ika꞉ weleke ana꞉ pia꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ mina꞉pa꞉lalimikie.
Kutupa enisolo ma꞉nda꞉ oli hepeni nanema꞉ hao holopolo ipulu ipika꞉ kiki pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ mo honiki na wiki naku tieke kiakena꞉ pota꞉na꞉ ki make ka꞉nda꞉ tieke piki seni miniki epea꞉eki handoa꞉me.
Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo hande popake itiki hake sita꞉ hande ambisanake hao haya꞉ keto kotota꞉ hande Depolo o Sadani la꞉la꞉ aleta꞉ mina 1 daoseni bapi manuna꞉ senima꞉ tonkaeya꞉me.
Mo enisoloma꞉ta꞉ mo sita꞉ oni naku tieke kiake pa꞉ta꞉ yola꞉ mea loka꞉ hao a꞉mbo pambea꞉me. Pa ekipeke mo sima꞉ta꞉ do kenke paeyao haleme tapake ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ makeaama꞉na꞉ mo 1 daoseni bapimanu paeya꞉ka꞉na꞉ opolu baena꞉yeke pia꞉me. Koto hoki naneta꞉ nateleke hosiki siki ka꞉la꞉pa꞉ tapaalieke.
Kutupa kini seamanu handoa꞉me. Koto seana꞉ pitimi haliwekita꞉ pi yokaalu pulu pimi wele halea꞉me. Kutupa make mo hande Yesuma꞉ peneme yaeya꞉ ota꞉eki waleme ekina꞉ make Koda꞉na꞉ pi waleme ekina꞉ limiki wanda꞉halina꞉ temokomanu handoa꞉me. Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo hande sayale tieke hombeleke make ipiki manda꞉ meao wepimiki ale yaapo pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni na pimi make ika꞉ wenoko o popeke nane kikina꞉ mo sayalena꞉ maka na mimikime. Ikita꞉ paa da꞉ta hata꞉ 1 daoseni bapi manuna꞉ Ketiso ame̱le̱ kini pita꞉ handeteke haememe.
Do ekita꞉ ota꞉ titina꞉ homa꞉la꞉eki mea tiaasa꞉ekie. Mo mandane wopu homemeke wanda꞉hali paeyaota꞉ a̱i̱ na da꞉ta tiao haemepate mo 1 daoseni bapimanu hoki nane detena꞉ pia꞉me.
Mo mandane homeme wanda꞉halimanu do titina꞉ mea tiaasa꞉eki pa꞉ta꞉ apa꞉taemeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ ika꞉ta꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homena꞉ laa yako pina꞉ lelieke. Mo yaapo peao homa꞉la꞉ ekima꞉ta꞉ iki wataapeketa꞉ honkopu na ula꞉me. Ikita꞉ Koda꞉ pita꞉ Ketiso yaapona꞉ yeni peaasa꞉ haliweki hata꞉ 1 daoseni bapimanu ipiki ame̱le̱ handeteke halimikie.
Mo 1 daoseni bapimanu paeya꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ mo Sadanita꞉ ipika꞉ dipula pila꞉eki ka꞉la꞉pa꞉ tapaalieke.
Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ mo kenke honiki honiki paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ hala꞉ tapake paeyao makealieke. Kotota꞉ Koko pita꞉ Meikoko leke tapakee. Sadanima꞉ta꞉ paeyao a꞉nda꞉na꞉ hatuku ipilieke. Mo tapaketa꞉ mo dawala hou manuma꞉ handilimikie.
Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ kenke tieke tumbaaso hata꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ mombeleme alena꞉ make Koda꞉na꞉ pukima꞉ homa꞉la꞉ daoni make pua popei yaememe. Pate ti uleke oli hepeni nanema꞉ a꞉pa lopaa paeyao hoeyaeya꞉me.
Kutupa mo wanda꞉hali makeaeya꞉ Sadanita꞉ oni ti uleke kiake make titipupiki lanka꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ biki solopa pa꞉ta꞉ yola꞉ mea lopaeya꞉me. Kotota꞉ amba꞉ hande sayale tieke hombeleke make mo makeaaso potopede hali make lopala꞉ pa꞉ta꞉e. Kutupa ikita꞉ timba꞉ ala꞉eki make natepa yolao hoto paeyao puki tandama꞉ homo halimikie.
Kutupa mo hakepiki kini sea tieke pita꞉ mo seana꞉ pila꞉ hali yaapo handoa꞉me. Kutupa mo kenke ya yaapota꞉ ipika꞉ leke popelekena꞉ na haena꞉ loluekema꞉ pa pindipa pualu pitolo hata꞉ alupaepeme.
Kutupa mo homemeke wanda꞉hali aneke make natehali make paeyao mandakena꞉ mo kini seana꞉ puki tikitiki haemeeki handoa꞉me. Buka manuta꞉ lumbia꞉me. Kutupa buka ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ mo da꞉ta꞉la꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ buka lumbia꞉me. Mo homemeke wanda꞉hali paeyaota꞉ mo buka manuna꞉ lao wieke tupa꞉ ika꞉ pimiki tupa꞉ siki kone ma̱leke lia telipia꞉me.
Kutupa mo dawalama꞉ ipiki pa꞉ta꞉ homemeke wanda꞉hali halea꞉me. Kutupa homa꞉la꞉ ekima꞉ make mo homo hala꞉ kenkema꞉ make ipilika꞉ wia haepe toko halepeme. Kutupa paeyaota꞉ ika꞉ pimiki tupa꞉ siki kone ana꞉na꞉ ma̱leke lia telipia꞉me.
Kutupa homa꞉la꞉eki pita꞉ homo hala꞉ kenke yaapota꞉ oni ti uleke pa꞉ta꞉ yola꞉ mea lopaeya꞉me. Do ti uleke kiaketa꞉ yaapo peao homa꞉la꞉ekie.
Kutupa make ma꞉nda꞉ epi ipika꞉ bikita꞉ mo da꞉ta꞉la꞉ wanda꞉halina꞉ bukana꞉ na laeya꞉ someta꞉ oni ti uleke kiake pa꞉ta꞉ yola꞉ mea lopaeya꞉me.
Koto hoki naneta꞉ I̱ma꞉ panake hepeni pita꞉ panake kenke yaapo handoa꞉me. Titina꞉ hepeni pita꞉ kenke yaapota꞉ alupaeya꞉me. Kutupa mo dawala make loa꞉me.
Mo hande Yakopiki Daoni hande panake Diutuselemeta꞉ wanda꞉ma꞉ ipika꞉ haliki ma̱landi puluekema꞉ amu pea tikitiki yao ipulu pita꞉la꞉ tupa꞉ oli hepeni nanema꞉ Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ opolo epea꞉eki handoa꞉me.
Oli kini sea nanema꞉ pi ho̱la̱꞉make tiekema꞉ dupa lea꞉eki opua꞉me. Ameta꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ data꞉ wanda꞉hali ame̱le̱ hala꞉me. Ipikita꞉ iki ame̱le̱ hata꞉ mo wanda꞉halita꞉ ipika꞉ wanda꞉hali au lalieke. Koda꞉ ipikita꞉ mo wanda꞉hali ame̱le̱ halieke. Ipikita꞉ ika꞉ Koda꞉ halieke.
Ipikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ika꞉ e̱ pankekemanu honialieke. Koto pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ homa꞉la꞉eki pa na handilimikie. Kutupa puki tanda pitolo a꞉ta꞉ma꞉ homa꞉la꞉eki make e̱ ala꞉eki make tanda mina꞉la꞉eki make ota꞉ dia꞉ya꞉lieke. Mo amba꞉ haumanu paeyaota꞉ alu paeya꞉me laa lea꞉me.
Kutupa mo kini seana꞉ pitia꞉ halima꞉ alota꞉ Ameta꞉ I̱ma꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ paeyao panakeeki wepitolome lea꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ dupa alota꞉ Do ekita꞉ laaniae. Pa ekipeke do pi manuta꞉ ota꞉eki ya꞉la꞉ ekina꞉ make ota꞉ hone tu lapeke ya꞉la꞉ pie lea꞉me.
Kutupa ombu alota꞉ Ameta꞉ pu paela꞉me. I̱ta꞉ titina꞉ make sale nane makee. Kini pitolo make paeyaaso makee. Ma꞉nda꞉ epita꞉ ikali na꞉na꞉ma꞉ homea꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ I̱ma꞉ mo opa꞉la꞉ da꞉taasa꞉ ikalita꞉ na hambeke pa nena꞉ waleke halueke.
Ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ a꞉nda꞉ peaa bepolaasa꞉ hali haya꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ doeki mina꞉e. I̱ta꞉ ipika꞉ Koda꞉ halueke. Kutupa ipikita꞉ yaka weki au lalueke.
Pate hone pamboneke tapake make ba꞉sa꞉ piteleme tapake make ata꞉ka꞉ peaaseme tapake make honema꞉ kone hali lu homaaseme tapake make pake nalo loke apa꞉taaseme tapake make ti̱o̱ hau pu haleme tapake make toopi ti wepia ula꞉ ale pa꞉ta꞉ yeni pu haleme tapake make mo yayapiki pi lo haleme tapake make paeyaota꞉ ika꞉ hala꞉peke ya꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ oni ti uleke kiake make titipupiki lanka꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ biki solopa bu lo hala꞉ pa꞉ta꞉e. Koto hau pita꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ mo yaapo peao homa꞉la꞉ekie.
Mo hande paeyaaso watake hata꞉ ke handa꞉la꞉eki manuma꞉ tumbulu baake kawaso miniki haeme hande watake hata꞉ enisolo homekema꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ a꞉pa alota꞉ I̱ma꞉ mo hande Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ ma꞉la꞉ wanda꞉ walono epoe lea꞉me.
Mo Sipitidima꞉ I̱ tukiki pa꞉ta꞉ e pokolo hata꞉ mo enisoloma꞉ I̱ta꞉ ota꞉ oli pote tieke tumikina꞉ mea tia pea꞉me. Ipikana꞉ma꞉ mo panake Diutuseleme hande yakopiki daoni oli hepeni nane Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ hao holopolo epea꞉eki I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ walea꞉me.
Mo daonita꞉ Koda꞉na꞉ pa̱a̱ piti pa̱a̱ putia ipulu hata꞉ dia꞉sepa leke toopi seliapoma꞉ handa ala꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ na ta̱leke kalasima꞉ handeekeme.
Mo daonita꞉ hokulupiki pape tiekema꞉ popei yao pota꞉ kaketa꞉ paeyao kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo lombaya꞉me. Mo pota꞉ kake yalaota꞉ kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo enisoloma꞉ handeteke haememe. Mo pota꞉ kake manuna꞉ yalaota꞉ mo Isulai wanda꞉halina꞉ kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo tapakena꞉ biki laeya꞉me.
Mo nepokomanu yalaota꞉ pota꞉kake tepo lo lombaya꞉me. Nate opa꞉la꞉ naneta꞉ pota꞉ kake tepo lombaya꞉me. Nepoko yaapo nane make pota꞉ kake tepo tepo lo lombaya꞉me. Oni nate pamba꞉la꞉ nane make pota꞉ kake tepo lombaya꞉me.
Mo daonina꞉ papeta꞉ kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo pinki nonopiki toopi oto tiekena꞉ noko peekeme. Koto toopi manuna꞉ta꞉ mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikikina꞉ aposolo hali kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapona꞉ biki laeya꞉me.
Mo I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ pi la kia꞉ enisolota꞉ mo daoni make ipika꞉ pota꞉ kakemanu make ipika꞉ pape pa꞉la꞉eki make paeyao tombo muluekema꞉ mo koloma꞉ wepiki tombo mina꞉la꞉ tolo miniki haya꞉me.
Mo daonina꞉ petipeke maka make mo hokulu maka make ota꞉ homeke make pa꞉la꞉me. Mo enisoloma꞉ ipika꞉ tombo mina꞉la꞉ doloma꞉ mo daonina꞉ tombo mia꞉me. Mo daonita꞉ 2 daosenina꞉ 400 kilomida ota꞉ hokulu pea make petipeke ya꞉la꞉eki make olina꞉ hokulu pa꞉la꞉eki make homeke hau kone piekeme.
Kutupa mo enisoloma꞉ ombu mo daonina꞉ pape polopala꞉eki tombo mia꞉pate ota꞉ 60 mida mia꞉me. Mo tombo mina꞉la꞉ alena꞉ hokulu piki ekita꞉ ota꞉ ana꞉na꞉ kone tombo mia꞉me.
Mo papeta꞉ dia꞉sepa leke toopima꞉ wepiekeme. Kutupa mo daonita꞉ koloma꞉ handa ala꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ na ta̱leke kalasima꞉ handea꞉me.
Mo daonina꞉ papena꞉ pinki toopi manuna꞉ta꞉ ane mone seliapopiki toopi manuma꞉ popei yao ota꞉ lu liaeyekeme. Titina꞉ toopi pinkita꞉ biki dia꞉sepa yekeme. Yaapo peao toopi pinkina꞉ bikita꞉ sa꞉paeya yekeme. Tepo peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ a꞉keidi yekeme. Tonko peao ekita꞉ ambuma꞉ handeke au leke toopi biki emulolidi yekeme.
Yunki peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ onkisi yekeme. Yunki mindiki hata꞉ peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ kaniliani yekeme. Watake hata꞉ peao ekita꞉ hamipiki toopi biki kotisalaedi yekeme. Ketepo peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ betili yekeme. No̱i̱ peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ topa꞉si yekeme. Kiki yaapo peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ kotisapoteisi yekeme. Kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ homeke peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ dieisini yekeme. Kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo peao ekina꞉ bikita꞉ a꞉metisi yekeme.
Mo kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo pota꞉ kake manuta꞉ kiki yaapona꞉ ankena꞉ yaapo sekete hapekemanu yekeme. Mo pota꞉ kake manuna꞉ yalaota꞉ mo sekete hapekema꞉ wepuma꞉ wepuma꞉ piekeme. Mo daonina꞉ pota꞉ta꞉ aleta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ na taleke kalasima꞉ handeke koloma꞉ pilaeyekeme.
I̱ma꞉ta꞉ mo daoni pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ tembolo da na handoa꞉me. Pa ekipeke mo Aneke Tekehali Koda꞉ pita꞉ mo hande Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki yaapota꞉ mo tembolo da yekeme.
Mo daonina꞉ta꞉ nate o kaisepo ma꞉nda꞉ pa̱a̱ pealuekema꞉ opa꞉peke na ya꞉me. Pa ekipeke mo Koda꞉na꞉ au la꞉la꞉ pa̱a̱ta꞉ koto pa꞉ta꞉ pa̱a̱ pu hala꞉me. Kutupa mo daonina꞉ ola꞉paketa꞉ mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki ya꞉me.
Koto kenke wanda꞉halita꞉ mo daonina꞉ pa̱a̱na꞉ pomilimikie. Kutupa mo kenkena꞉ kini manuma꞉ta꞉ ika꞉ hamoko ale manuta꞉ ipiki pa꞉ta꞉ mea ipilimikie.
Mo daonina꞉ pota꞉ kake manuta꞉ nate paeyao pa lomba꞉pa wilieke. Ota꞉ na pokilieke. Pa ekipeke koto pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ timba꞉ ala꞉eki ota꞉ dia꞉ya꞉lieke.
Mo kenkena꞉ aneke make hamoko ale paeyaota꞉ mo daoni pa꞉ta꞉ mea ipilimikie.
Pate mo ha̱i̱ piki ala꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ koto daoni pa꞉ta꞉ na honda꞉ pambilieke. Koto tupa꞉ kone ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ yaala꞉piki haumanu pu o yayapiki pi lo hala꞉ some make na honda꞉ pambilieke. Mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki ipika꞉ da꞉ta꞉la꞉ tapakena꞉ biki ula꞉ bukana꞉ biki laala꞉ wanda꞉hali homeke koto daoni pa꞉ta꞉ honda꞉ pambilimikie.
Mo enisoloma꞉ta꞉ ala꞉ta꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ na ta̱leke kalasima꞉ handeke da꞉ta꞉la꞉eki kita꞉la꞉ ikali yopulu hala꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ walea꞉me. Mo ikalita꞉ oli Koda꞉ pita꞉ Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki yaapona꞉ kini sea pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ epea꞉me.
Kutupa mo ikalita꞉ mo daonina꞉ pota꞉ tukikina꞉ yapea꞉me. Mo ikali tea꞉ yaapona꞉ta꞉ hande da꞉ta꞉la꞉eki kita꞉la꞉ ti opo hala꞉me. Mo tima꞉ta꞉ bapi homekena꞉ta꞉ sumba꞉ homeke homeke yalao kiliki a꞉eya꞉tiki pu hala꞉me. Kutupa ipika꞉ katake manuta꞉ mo tapake ta꞉ta꞉ ta꞉ta꞉ paeyaona꞉ epeaasa꞉ekie.
Mo Koda꞉ma꞉ta꞉ hoeyaena꞉ laa ma̱leke lia ula꞉ ale ma꞉nda꞉ta꞉ koto daoni pa꞉ta꞉ ota꞉ na wilieke. Mo Koda꞉ pita꞉ mo Sipisipi Ma꞉na꞉ Ikiki yaapona꞉ kini seata꞉ koto daoni pa꞉ta꞉ wilieke. Kutupa ipika꞉ e pokaaseme wanda꞉halita꞉ ipiki pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pu halimikie.
Ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ ipika꞉ leke popeleke handaa make ipika꞉ bikita꞉ ika꞉ wenokonina꞉ laalimikie.
Koto pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ timba꞉ ala꞉eki ota꞉ dia꞉yalo hata꞉ ola꞉pake make natena꞉ pa̱a̱ make na weilimikie. Pa ekipeke mo Tekehali Koda꞉ta꞉ ika꞉ pa̱a̱ halieke. Kutupa ikana꞉ma꞉ta꞉ kinimanu pita꞉ hoto paeyao handeteke hao halimikie.
Kutupa mo enisoloma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ alota꞉ Do pi manuta꞉ ota꞉eki ya꞉la꞉ ekina꞉ hone tu lapeke ya꞉la꞉me. Kutupa hande potopede haliweki pa꞉ta꞉ Sipitidi halo pa꞉la꞉ Tekehali Koda꞉ma꞉ mo ipika꞉ e pokaaseme haliweki pa꞉ta꞉ ame do koto kone pulu pa꞉la꞉ ekimanu walena꞉yeke ipika꞉ enisolo tapaala꞉me lea꞉me.
Yesuma꞉ alota꞉ Opie. I̱ta꞉ teke pa꞉ta꞉ ipulume. Do buka pa꞉ta꞉ ula꞉ wetepena꞉ pulu pa꞉la꞉ pimanu pa꞉ta꞉ opua pu haleme wanda꞉halita꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homilimikie.
I̱ Dionima꞉ do hau paeyao handaa make opua꞉me. Kutupa do haumanu handa make opu paeyaota꞉ I̱ta꞉ do haumanu walea꞉ enisolona꞉ anketeke pa꞉ta꞉ lopa ipiki pa꞉ta꞉ panda꞉puniao yeiya꞉ laaluekema꞉ pitua꞉pate
ipikana꞉ma꞉ I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ alota꞉ Kotoeki na pia꞉pema laata꞉ I̱ta꞉ e pokaaso naka꞉ yankekee. Kutupa make mo hande naka꞉ potopede kame manuna꞉ make do bukana꞉ ula꞉ wapena꞉ opua pita꞉la꞉ wanda꞉hali paeyaona꞉ yankeke kone halome. Koda꞉ pa꞉ta꞉ homeke yeiya꞉ laaso hata꞉ yeni pu hapeke laa lea꞉me.
Kutupa I̱ pa꞉ta꞉ ombu alota꞉ Do bukana꞉ la꞉ ula꞉ wetepena꞉ pulu pa꞉la꞉ pi manuta꞉ na a꞉mbao wia꞉peke. Pa ekipeke do haumanu paeyaona꞉ pulu pa꞉la꞉ nateta꞉ teke pa꞉ta꞉ ya꞉la꞉me.
Epi a꞉nda꞉ hoke temoko haeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ota꞉ hoke hau homeke pa pu hapeke. Epi a꞉nda꞉ ha̱i̱piki some pu haeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ota꞉ ha̱i̱piki hau homeke pa pu hapeke. Epi a꞉nda꞉ epeke some haeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ota꞉ epeke hau homeke pa pu hapeke. Kutupa epi a꞉nda꞉ yakopiki some haeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ ota꞉ yako piki hau homeke pa pu hapeke.
Yesuma꞉ alota꞉ Opie. I̱ta꞉ teke pa꞉ta꞉ ipulu hata꞉ ika꞉ yenkita꞉ ika꞉ homeke homeke peleme tupa꞉ kone ana꞉na꞉ haluekema꞉ I̱ma꞉ mo halo polo alemanu mea ipulume.
I̱ta꞉ titina꞉ make sale nane makee. Kini pitolo make paeyaaso makee laa lea꞉me.
Epi amedama꞉ ika꞉ aka꞉manu tanda꞉pa hake peaemeka꞉na꞉ta꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homena꞉e. Ikita꞉ mo hande da꞉ta꞉la꞉eki hala꞉la꞉ tina꞉ kiliki nena꞉ make mo daonina꞉ pota꞉ kake pa꞉ta꞉ yama꞉ pena꞉ make waleke halieke.
Pate mo ata꞉ka꞉ peaaseme tapake make ti̱o̱ hau pu haleme tapake make pake nalo loke apa꞉taaseme tapake make honema꞉ kone hali lu homaaseme tapake make toopi ti wepia꞉ ula꞉ ale pa꞉ta꞉ yeni hau pu haleme tapake make yayapiki ekina꞉ ta꞉na꞉ma꞉ homa pu haleme tapake make paeyao sikita꞉ mo daoni tea꞉na꞉ hama꞉ nane halememe.
I̱ta꞉ Yesuma꞉ do hau manuta꞉ iki siosimanu haleme wanda꞉hali pa꞉ta꞉ lawaena꞉ yaka enisolo tapaalome. Deipidita꞉ yaka apa꞉mei halie. I̱ta꞉ mo hande da ka꞉la꞉paaso opa꞉la꞉ pa̱a̱ tieke piki hombulanka꞉e laa lea꞉me.
Mo Sipitidi pita꞉ mo hali panake pula꞉ wanda꞉ yaapoma꞉ alota꞉ Epoe ala꞉me. Do pi opilimi tapake paeyaoma꞉ make Epoe lapa꞉peke ya꞉lieke. Ikali na꞉na꞉ma꞉ homele some epita꞉ do da꞉taapeke ya꞉la꞉ ikalita꞉ pa hameke kita꞉la꞉ekie laa mea꞉peke ya꞉la꞉me. Dota꞉ ma꞉nda꞉ epi hone pa꞉la꞉ somena꞉ loa꞉me lea꞉me.
I̱ta꞉ Dionima꞉ do la꞉ ula꞉ wetepena꞉ pulu pa꞉la꞉ pimanu opiteleme wanda꞉hali pa꞉ta꞉ kinki pita꞉la꞉ pi dupa alome. Ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ do pimanu pa꞉ta꞉ pi ma꞉nda꞉ apa꞉taeya꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ Koda꞉ma꞉ koto some ipika꞉ panisi pa꞉ta꞉ta꞉ do bukana꞉ la꞉la꞉ kemanu handa꞉pekeeki apa꞉taalieke.
Kutupa ma꞉nda꞉ epima꞉ do bukana꞉ ula꞉ wetepena꞉ pulu pa꞉la꞉ pimanu ma꞉nda꞉ mea baeya꞉ka꞉na꞉ta꞉ kota꞉ koto some ipika꞉ mo da꞉ta꞉la꞉eki hala꞉peke ya꞉la꞉ tina꞉ kiliki mulupa꞉la꞉ yenkina꞉ putupilikita꞉ pao mea make mo hande yakopiki daoni pua hapeke ya꞉la꞉eki make Koda꞉ma꞉ pao milieke. Do bukana꞉ la꞉la꞉ ekina꞉ loa꞉me.
Do wape pa꞉la꞉ pi manuta꞉ ota꞉ pie laa la꞉ wita꞉la꞉ somema꞉ alota꞉ Aowe. Ota꞉ a꞉pa꞉la꞉me. I̱ta꞉ teke pa꞉ta꞉ ipulume lea꞉me. Koto ekina꞉ta꞉ kutu pia꞉peke. Tekehali Yesuo. Epoe.
Tekehali Yesuna꞉ a꞉ta꞉ma꞉ homolo tamba꞉ mina꞉la꞉ ekita꞉ iki paeyao pa꞉ta꞉ wina꞉e.
